\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ exponents\ without\ overflowing\ or\ underflowing\ in\ intermediate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ computations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Since\ 'a'\ and\ the\ output\ can\ be\ denormal,\ the\ maximum\ range\ of\ 'exponent'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ consider\ for\ a\ float\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/255-\/23\ -\/>\ 255+23}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Below\ -\/278\ any\ finite\ float\ 'a'\ will\ become\ zero,\ and\ above\ +278\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ finite\ float\ will\ become\ inf,\ including\ when\ 'a'\ is\ the\ smallest\ possible\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ denormal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Unfortunately,\ 2\string^(278)\ cannot\ be\ represented\ using\ either\ one\ or\ two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ finite\ normal\ floats,\ so\ we\ must\ split\ the\ scale\ factor\ into\ at\ least}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ three\ parts.\ It\ turns\ out\ to\ be\ faster\ to\ split\ 'exponent'\ into\ four}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ factors,\ since\ [exponent>>2]\ is\ much\ faster\ to\ compute\ that\ [exponent/3].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Set\ e\ =\ min(max(exponent,\ -\/278),\ 278);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ b\ =\ floor(e/4);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ out\ =\ ((((a\ *\ 2\string^(b))\ *\ 2\string^(b))\ *\ 2\string^(b))\ *\ 2\string^(e-\/3*b))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ will\ avoid\ any\ intermediate\ overflows\ and\ correctly\ handle\ 0,\ inf,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NaN\ cases.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00769\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Computes\ the\ principal\ sqrt\ of\ the\ complex\ numbers\ in\ the\ input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00770\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00771\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ example,\ for\ packets\ containing\ 2\ complex\ numbers\ stored\ in\ interleaved\ format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00772\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ a\ =\ [a0,\ a1]\ =\ [x0,\ y0,\ x1,\ y1],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00773\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ where\ x0\ =\ real(a0),\ y0\ =\ imag(a0)\ etc.,\ this\ function\ returns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00774\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ b\ =\ [b0,\ b1]\ =\ [u0,\ v0,\ u1,\ v1],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00775\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ such\ that\ b0\string^2\ =\ a0,\ b1\string^2\ =\ a1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ derive\ the\ formula\ for\ the\ complex\ square\ roots,\ let's\ consider\ the\ equation\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ single\ complex\ square\ root\ of\ the\ number\ x\ +\ i*y.\ We\ want\ to\ find\ real\ numbers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ u\ and\ v\ such\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00780\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ (u\ +\ i*v)\string^2\ =\ x\ +\ i*y\ \ <=>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00781\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ u\string^2\ -\/\ v\string^2\ +\ i*2*u*v\ =\ x\ +\ i*v.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00782\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ By\ equating\ the\ real\ and\ imaginary\ parts\ we\ get:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00783\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ u\string^2\ -\/\ v\string^2\ =\ x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00784\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ 2*u*v\ =\ y.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00785\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00786\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ x\ >=\ 0,\ this\ has\ the\ numerically\ stable\ solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00787\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ u\ =\ sqrt(0.5\ *\ (x\ +\ sqrt(x\string^2\ +\ y\string^2)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00788\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ v\ =\ 0.5\ *\ (y\ /\ u)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00789\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ for\ x\ <\ 0,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00790\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ v\ =\ sign(y)\ *\ sqrt(0.5\ *\ (-\/x\ +\ sqrt(x\string^2\ +\ y\string^2)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00791\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ u\ =\ 0.5\ *\ (y\ /\ v)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00792\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00793\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ To\ avoid\ unnecessary\ over-\/\ and\ underflow,\ we\ compute\ sqrt(x\string^2\ +\ y\string^2)\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00794\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ l\ =\ max(|x|,\ |y|)\ *\ sqrt(1\ +\ (min(|x|,\ |y|)\ /\ max(|x|,\ |y|))\string^2)\ ,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00795\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00796\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ the\ following,\ without\ lack\ of\ generality,\ we\ have\ annotated\ the\ code,\ assuming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00797\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ the\ input\ is\ a\ packet\ of\ 2\ complex\ numbers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00798\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00799\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Step\ 1.\ Compute\ l\ =\ [l0,\ l0,\ l1,\ l1],\ where}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00801\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ avoid\ over-\/\ and\ underflow,\ we\ use\ the\ stable\ formula\ for\ each\ hypotenuse}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00803\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ where\ max0\ =\ max(|x0|,\ |y0|),\ min0\ =\ min(|x0|,\ |y0|),\ and\ similarly\ for\ l1.}}
